md:max-w-[calc(100%_-var(--sidebar-width))]" data-pagefind-body=""><div class="hidden sm:block relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 "><nav aria-label="Breadcrumb" class="py-4 max-w-4xl md:px-4 mb-2"><ol class="flex items-center text-sm"><li><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-started/quickstarts">Home</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/monitoring">Monitor your data</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><span class="font-semibold">Service Data Sources</span></li></ol></nav></div><div class="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]"><div class="max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="service-data-sources" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">Service data sources<a class="headerlink" href="#service-data-sources" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V8z"></path><path d="M14 2v6h6M16 13H8M16 17H8M10 9H8"></path></svg><span>Copy as MD</span></button><button class="flex items-center justify-center px-2 py-1.5 text-sm text-v-text-01 border-l border-v-border-02 min-w-[32px]" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-3 h-3 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><p>Tinybird provides Service data sources that you can use to inspect what&#x27;s going on in your Tinybird account, diagnose issues, monitor usage, and so on.</p><p>For example, you can get real time stats about API calls or a log of every operation over your data sources. This is similar to using system tables in a database, although Service data sources contain information about the usage of the service itself.</p><p>Queries made to Service data sources are free of charge and don&#x27;t count towards your usage. However, calls to API endpoints that use Service data sources do count towards API rate limits. See <a href="../pricing">Billing</a>.</p><h2 id="considerations" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Considerations<a class="headerlink" href="#considerations" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><ul><li>You can&#x27;t use Service data sources in materialized view queries.</li><li>Pass dynamic query parameters to API endpoints to then query Service data sources.</li><li>You can only query Organization-level Service data sources if you&#x27;re an administrator. See <a href="../administration/organizations#consumption-overview">Consumption overview</a>.</li></ul><h2 id="service-data-sources" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Service data sources<a class="headerlink" href="#service-data-sources" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>The following Service data sources are available.</p><h3 id="tinybird-pipe-stats-rt" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.pipe_stats_rt<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-pipe-stats-rt" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Contains information about all requests made to your <a href="../work-with-data/publish-data/endpoints">API endpoints</a> in real time. This data source has a TTL of 7 days. If you need to query data older than 7 days you must use the aggregated by day data available at <a href="#tinybird-pipe-stats">tinybird.pipe_stats</a>.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Calls made against Service data sources are not logged and don&#x27;t count towards usage limits.</p></div></div><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th width="22%">Type </th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>start_datetime</code></td><td><code>DateTime</code></td><td>API call start date and time.</td></tr><tr><td><code>pipe_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>pipe Id as returned in our <a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api">pipes API</a> (<code>query_api</code> in case it&#x27;s a Query API request).</td></tr><tr><td><code>pipe_name</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>pipe name as returned in our  <a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api">pipes API</a> (<code>query_api</code> in case it&#x27;s a Query API request).</td></tr><tr><td><code>duration</code></td><td><code>Float</code></td><td>API call duration, in seconds.</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_bytes</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>API call read data, in bytes.</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_rows</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>API call rows read.</td></tr><tr><td><code>result_rows</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Rows returned by the API call.</td></tr><tr><td><code>url</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>URL (<code>token</code> param is removed for security reasons).</td></tr><tr><td><code>error</code></td><td><code>UInt8</code></td><td><code>1</code> if query returned error, else <code>0</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>request_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>API call identifier returned in <code>x-request-id</code> header. Format is ULID string.</td></tr><tr><td><code>token</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>API call token identifier used.</td></tr><tr><td><code>token_name</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>API call token name used.</td></tr><tr><td><code>status_code</code></td><td><code>Int32</code></td><td>API call returned status code.</td></tr><tr><td><code>method</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>API call method POST or GET.</td></tr><tr><td><code>parameters</code></td><td><code>Map(String, String)</code></td><td>API call parameters used.</td></tr><tr><td><code>release</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Semantic version of the release (deprecated).</td></tr><tr><td><code>user_agent</code></td><td><code>Nullable(String)</code></td><td>User Agent HTTP header from the request.</td></tr><tr><td><code>resource_tags</code></td><td><code>Array(String)</code></td><td>Tags associated with the pipe when the request was made.</td></tr><tr><td><code>cpu_time</code></td><td><code>Float</code></td><td>CPU time used by the query, in seconds.</td></tr><tr><td><code>memory_usage</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Memory consumption by the query, in bytes. High memory usage indicates the query may not be optimized efficiently.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h3 id="tinybird-pipe-stats" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.pipe_stats<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-pipe-stats" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Aggregates the request stats in <a href="#tinybird-pipe-stats-rt">tinybird.pipe_stats_rt</a> by day.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Calls made against Service data sources are not logged and don&#x27;t count towards usage limits.</p></div></div><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>date</code></td><td><code>Date</code></td><td>Request date and time.</td></tr><tr><td><code>pipe_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>pipe Id as returned in our <a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api">pipes API</a>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>pipe_name</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Name of the pipe.</td></tr><tr><td><code>view_count</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Request count.</td></tr><tr><td><code>error_count</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Number of requests with error.</td></tr><tr><td><code>avg_duration_state</code></td><td><code>AggregateFunction(avg, Float32)</code></td><td>Average duration state, in seconds (see <a href="#querying-state-columns">Querying _state columns</a>).</td></tr><tr><td><code>quantile_timing_state</code></td><td><code>AggregateFunction(quantilesTiming(0.9, 0.95, 0.99), Float64)</code></td><td>0.9, 0.95 and 0.99 quantiles state. Time, in milliseconds (see <a href="#querying-state-columns">Querying _state columns</a>).</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_bytes_sum</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Total bytes read.</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_rows_sum</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Total rows read.</td></tr><tr><td><code>resource_tags</code></td><td><code>Array(String)</code></td><td>All the tags associated with the resource when the aggregated requests were made.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h3 id="tinybird-bi-stats-rt" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.bi_stats_rt<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-bi-stats-rt" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>This data source has a TTL of 7 days. If you need to query data older than 7 days you must use the aggregated by day data available at <a href="#tinybird-bi-stats">tinybird.bi_stats</a>.</p></div></div><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>start_datetime</code></td><td><code>DateTime</code></td><td>Query start timestamp.</td></tr><tr><td><code>query</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Executed query.</td></tr><tr><td><code>query_normalized</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Normalized executed query. This is the pattern of the query, without literals. Useful to analyze usage patterns.</td></tr><tr><td><code>error_code</code></td><td><code>Int32</code></td><td>Error code, if any. <code>0</code> on normal execution.</td></tr><tr><td><code>error</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Error description, if any. Empty otherwise.</td></tr><tr><td><code>duration</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Query duration, in milliseconds.</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_rows</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Read rows.</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_bytes</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Read bytes.</td></tr><tr><td><code>result_rows</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Total rows returned.</td></tr><tr><td><code>result_bytes</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Total bytes returned.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h3 id="tinybird-bi-stats" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.bi_stats<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-bi-stats" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Aggregates the stats in <a href="#tinybird-bi-stats-rt">tinybird.bi_stats_rt</a> by day.</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th width="20%">Field </th><th width="20%">Type </th><th width="60%">Description </th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>date</code></td><td><code>Date</code></td><td>Stats date.</td></tr><tr><td><code>database</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Database identifier.</td></tr><tr><td><code>query_normalized</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Normalized executed query. This is the pattern of the query, without literals. Useful to analyze usage patterns.</td></tr><tr><td><code>view_count</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Requests count.</td></tr><tr><td><code>error_count</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Error count.</td></tr><tr><td><code>avg_duration_state</code></td><td><code>AggregateFunction(avg, Float32)</code></td><td>Average duration state, in milliseconds (see <a href="#querying-state-columns">Querying _state columns</a>).</td></tr><tr><td><code>quantile_timing_state</code></td><td><code>AggregateFunction(quantilesTiming(0.9, 0.95, 0.99), Float64)</code></td><td>0.9, 0.95 and 0.99 quantiles state. Time, in milliseconds (see <a href="#querying-state-columns">Querying _state columns</a>).</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_bytes_sum</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Total bytes read.</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_rows_sum</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Total rows read.</td></tr><tr><td><code>avg_result_rows_state</code></td><td><code>AggregateFunction(avg, Float32)</code></td><td>Total bytes returned state (see <a href="#querying-state-columns">Querying _state columns</a>).</td></tr><tr><td><code>avg_result_bytes_state</code></td><td><code>AggregateFunction(avg, Float32)</code></td><td>Total rows returned state (see <a href="#querying-state-columns">Querying _state columns</a>).</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h3 id="tinybird-block-log" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.block_log<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-block-log" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The data source contains details about how Tinybird ingests data into your data sources. You can use this Service data source to spot problematic parts of your data.</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>timestamp</code></td><td><code>DateTime</code></td><td>Date and time of the block ingestion.</td></tr><tr><td><code>import_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Id of the import operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>job_id</code></td><td><code>Nullable(String)</code></td><td>Id of the job that ingested the block of data, if it was ingested by URL. In this case, <code>import_id</code> and <code>job_id</code> must have the same value.</td></tr><tr><td><code>request_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Id of the request that performed the operation. In this case, <code>import_id</code> and <code>job_id</code> must have the same value. Format is ULID string.</td></tr><tr><td><code>source</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Either the URL or <code>stream</code> or <code>body</code> keywords.</td></tr><tr><td><code>block_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Block identifier. You can cross this with the <code>blocks_ids</code> column from the <a href="#tinybird-datasources-ops-log">tinybird.datasources_ops_log</a> Service data source.</td></tr><tr><td><code>status</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td><code>done</code> | <code>error</code>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>datasource_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>data source consistent id.</td></tr><tr><td><code>datasource_name</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>data source name when the block was ingested.</td></tr><tr><td><code>start_offset</code></td><td><code>Nullable(Int64)</code></td><td>The starting byte of the block, if the ingestion was split, where this block started.</td></tr><tr><td><code>end_offset</code></td><td><code>Nullable(Int64)</code></td><td>If split, the ending byte of the block.</td></tr><tr><td><code>rows</code></td><td><code>Nullable(Int32)</code></td><td>How many rows it ingested.</td></tr><tr><td><code>parser</code></td><td><code>Nullable(String)</code></td><td>Whether the native block parser or falling back to row by row parsing is used.</td></tr><tr><td><code>quarantine_lines</code></td><td><code>Nullable(UInt32)</code></td><td>If any, how many rows went into the quarantine data source.</td></tr><tr><td><code>empty_lines</code></td><td><code>Nullable(UInt32)</code></td><td>If any, how many empty lines were skipped.</td></tr><tr><td><code>bytes</code></td><td><code>Nullable(UInt32)</code></td><td>How many bytes the block had.</td></tr><tr><td><code>processing_time</code></td><td><code>Nullable(Float32)</code></td><td>How long it took, in seconds.</td></tr><tr><td><code>processing_error</code></td><td><code>Nullable(String)</code></td><td>Detailed message in case of error.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>When Tinybird ingests data from a URL, it splits the download in several requests, resulting in different ingestion blocks. The same happens when the data upload happens with a multipart request.</p></div></div><h3 id="tinybird-datasources-ops-log" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.datasources_ops_log<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-datasources-ops-log" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Contains all operations performed to your data sources. Tinybird tracks the following operations:</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Event</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>create</code></td><td>A data source is created.</td></tr><tr><td><code>append</code></td><td>Append operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>append-hfi</code></td><td>Append operation using the <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/events-api">High-frequency Ingestion API</a>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>append-kafka</code></td><td>Append operation using the <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka">Kafka Connector</a>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>replace</code></td><td>A replace operation took place in the data source.</td></tr><tr><td><code>delete</code></td><td>A data source is deleted.</td></tr><tr><td><code>delete_data</code></td><td>A delete operation took place in the data source.</td></tr><tr><td><code>truncate</code></td><td>A truncate operation took place in the data source.</td></tr><tr><td><code>rename</code></td><td>The data source was renamed.</td></tr><tr><td><code>populateview-queued</code></td><td>A populate operation was queued for execution.</td></tr><tr><td><code>populateview</code></td><td>A finished populate operation (up to 8 hours after it started).</td></tr><tr><td><code>copy</code></td><td>A copy operation took place in the data source.</td></tr><tr><td><code>alter</code></td><td>An alter operation took place in the data source.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Materializations are logged with same <code>event_type</code> and <code>operation_id</code> as the operation that triggers them. You can track the materialization pipe with <code>pipe_id</code> and <code>pipe_name</code>.</p></div></div><p>Tinybird logs all operations with the following information in this data source:</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>timestamp</code></td><td><code>DateTime</code></td><td>Date and time when the operation started.</td></tr><tr><td><code>event_type</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Operation being logged.</td></tr><tr><td><code>operation_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Groups rows affected by the same operation. Useful for checking materializations triggered by an append operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>datasource_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Id of your data source. The data source id is consistent after renaming operations. You should use the id when you want to track name changes.</td></tr><tr><td><code>datasource_name</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Name of your data source when the operation happened.</td></tr><tr><td><code>result</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td><code>ok</code> | <code>error</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>elapsed_time</code></td><td><code>Float32</code></td><td>How much time the operation took, in seconds.</td></tr><tr><td><code>error</code></td><td><code>Nullable(String)</code></td><td>Detailed error message if the result was error.</td></tr><tr><td><code>import_id</code></td><td><code>Nullable(String)</code></td><td>Id of the import operation, if data has been ingested using one of the following operations: <code>create</code>, <code>append</code> or <code>replace</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>job_id</code></td><td><code>Nullable(String)</code></td><td>Id of the job that performed the operation, if any. If data has been ingested, <code>import_id</code> and <code>job_id</code> must have the same value.</td></tr><tr><td><code>request_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Id of the request that performed the operation. If data has been ingested, <code>import_id</code> and <code>request_id</code> must have the same value. Format is ULID string.</td></tr><tr><td><code>rows</code></td><td><code>Nullable(UInt64)</code></td><td>How many rows the operations affected. This depends on <code>event_type</code>: for the <code>append</code> event, how many rows got inserted; for <code>delete</code> or <code>truncate</code> events, how many rows the data source had; for <code>replace</code>, how many rows the data source has after the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>rows_quarantine</code></td><td><code>Nullable(UInt64)</code></td><td>How many rows went into the quarantine data source, if any.</td></tr><tr><td><code>blocks_ids</code></td><td><code>Array(String)</code></td><td>List of blocks ids used for the operation. See the <a href="#tinybird-block-log">tinybird.block_log</a> Service data source for more details.</td></tr><tr><td><code>options</code></td><td><code>Nested(Names String, Values String)</code></td><td>Tinybird stores key-value pairs with extra information for some operations. For the <code>replace</code> event, Tinybird uses the <code>rows_before_replace</code> key to track how many rows the data source had before the replacement happened, the <code>replace_condition</code> key shows what condition was used. For <code>append</code> and <code>replace</code> events, Tinybird stores the data <code>source</code>, for example the URL, or body/stream keywords. For <code>rename</code> event, <code>old_name</code> and <code>new_name</code>. For <code>populateview</code> you can find there the whole populate <code>job</code> metadata as a JSON string. For <code>alter</code> events, Tinybird stores  <code>operations</code>, and dependent pipes as <code>dependencies</code> if they exist.</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_bytes</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Read bytes in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_rows</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Read rows in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>written_rows</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Written rows in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>written_bytes</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Written bytes in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>written_rows_quarantine</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Quarantined rows in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>written_bytes_quarantine</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Quarantined bytes in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>pipe_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>If present, materialization pipe id as returned in our <a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api">pipes API</a>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>pipe_name</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>If present, materialization pipe name as returned in our <a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api">pipes API</a>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>release</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Semantic version of the release (deprecated).</td></tr><tr><td><code>resource_tags</code></td><td><code>Array(String)</code></td><td>Tags associated with the pipe when the request was made.</td></tr><tr><td><code>cpu_time</code></td><td><code>Float32</code></td><td>CPU time used by the operation, in seconds.</td></tr><tr><td><code>memory_usage</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Memory consuptiom by the operation, in bytes.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h3 id="tinybird-datasource-ops-stats" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.datasource_ops_stats<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-datasource-ops-stats" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Data from <code>datasource_ops_log</code>, aggregated by day.</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>event_date</code></td><td><code>Date</code></td><td>Date of the event.</td></tr><tr><td><code>workspace_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Unique identifier for the workspace.</td></tr><tr><td><code>event_type</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Name of your data source.</td></tr><tr><td><code>pipe_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Identifier of the pipe.</td></tr><tr><td><code>pipe_name</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Name of the pipe.</td></tr><tr><td><code>error_count</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Number of requests with an error.</td></tr><tr><td><code>executions</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Number of executions.</td></tr><tr><td><code>avg_elapsed_time_state</code></td><td><code>Float32</code></td><td>Average time spent in elapsed state.</td></tr><tr><td><code>quantiles_state</code></td><td><code>Float32</code></td><td>0.9, 0.95 and 0.99 quantiles state. Time in milliseconds (see <a href="#querying-state-columns">Querying _state columns</a>).</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_bytes</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Read bytes in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_rows</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Read rows in the Sink operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>written_rows</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Written rows in the Sink operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>read_bytes</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Read bytes in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>written_bytes</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Written bytes in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>written_rows_quarantine</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Quarantined rows in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>written_bytes_quarantine</code></td><td><code>UInt64</code></td><td>Quarantined bytes in the operation.</td></tr><tr><td><code>resource_tags</code></td><td><code>Array(String)</code></td><td>Tags associated with the pipe when the request was made.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h3 id="tinybird-endpoint-errors" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.endpoint_errors<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-endpoint-errors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>It provides the last 30 days errors of your published endpoints. Tinybird logs all errors with additional information in this data source.</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>start_datetime</code></td><td><code>DateTime</code></td><td>Date and time when the API call started.</td></tr><tr><td><code>request_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>The id of the request that performed the operation. Format is ULID string.</td></tr><tr><td><code>pipe_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>If present, pipe id as returned in our <a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api">pipes API</a>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>pipe_name</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>If present, pipe name as returned in our <a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api">pipes API</a>.</td></tr><tr><td><code>params</code></td><td><code>Nullable(String)</code></td><td>URL query params included in the request.</td></tr><tr><td><code>url</code></td><td><code>Nullable(String)</code></td><td>URL pathname.</td></tr><tr><td><code>status_code</code></td><td><code>Nullable(Int32)</code></td><td>HTTP error code.</td></tr><tr><td><code>error</code></td><td><code>Nullable(String)</code></td><td>Error message.</td></tr><tr><td><code>resource_tags</code></td><td><code>Array(String)</code></td><td>Tags associated with the pipe when the request was made.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h3 id="tinybird-kafka-ops-log" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.kafka_ops_log<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-kafka-ops-log" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Contains all operations performed to your Kafka data sources during the last 30 days.</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>timestamp</code></td><td><code>DateTime</code></td><td>Date and time when the operation took place.</td></tr><tr><td><code>datasource_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Id of your data source. The data source id is consistent after renaming operations. You should use the id when you want to track name changes.</td></tr><tr><td><code>topic</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Kafka topic.</td></tr><tr><td><code>partition</code></td><td><code>Int16</code></td><td>Partition number, or <code>-1</code> for all partitions.</td></tr><tr><td><code>msg_type</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>&#x27;info&#x27; for regular messages, &#x27;warning&#x27; for issues related to the user&#x27;s Kafka cluster, deserialization or materialized views, and &#x27;error&#x27; for other issues.</td></tr><tr><td><code>lag</code></td><td><code>Int64</code></td><td>Number of messages behind for the partition. This is the difference between the high-water mark and the last commit offset.</td></tr><tr><td><code>processed_messages</code></td><td><code>Int32</code></td><td>Messages processed for a topic and partition.</td></tr><tr><td><code>processed_bytes</code></td><td><code>Int32</code></td><td>Amount of bytes processed.</td></tr><tr><td><code>committed_messages</code></td><td><code>Int32</code></td><td>Messages ingested for a topic and partition.</td></tr><tr><td><code>msg</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Information in the case of warnings or errors. Empty otherwise.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h3 id="tinybird-datasources-storage" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.datasources_storage<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-datasources-storage" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Contains stats about your data sources storage.</p><p>Tinybird logs maximum values per hour, the same as when it calculates storage consumption.</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>datasource_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Id of your data source. md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Event</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>init</code></td><td>First Release is created on Git live.</td></tr><tr><td><code>post</code></td><td>Resources from a commit are deployed to the live Release.</td></tr><tr><td><code>rollback</code></td><td>Rollback is done a previous Release is now data-pagefind-weight="8.0">tinybird.query_validator_log<a class="headerlink" href="#tinybird-query-validator-log" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Contains information about query validation executions for Pipes and Materialized Views in your Workspace.</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>host</code></td><td><code>LowCardinality(String)</code></td><td>Name of the host the query error message if the query failed.</td></tr><tr><td><code>query_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>ClickHouse query ID. For Pipe queries, this can be matched with <code>system.query_log</code>. For Materialized Views, it contains the qualified internal table name.</td></tr><tr><td><code>query</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>The full query.</td></tr><tr><td><code>fix_suggestion</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Optionally, a suggestion on how to fix the query.</td></tr><tr><td><code>run_validation</code></td><td><code>DateTime</code></td><td>The time when this query was validated.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Learn more about how to monitor your queries for validation in the <a href="./query-validation">guide</a>.</p></div></div><h2 id="query-state-columns" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Query _state columns<a class="headerlink" href="#query-state-columns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Several of the Service data sources include columns suffixed with <code>_state</code>. This suffix identifies columns with values that are in an intermediate aggregated state. When reading these columns, merge the intermediate states to get the final value.</p><p>To merge intermediate states, wrap the column in the original aggregation function and apply the <code>-Merge</code> combinator.</p><p>For example, to finalize the value of the <code>avg_duration_state</code> column, you use the <code>avgMerge</code> function:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="finalize the value for the avg_duration_state column">finalize the value for the avg_duration_state column</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
  date,
  avgMerge(avg_duration_state) avg_time,
  quantilesTimingMerge(0.9, 0.95, 0.99)(quantile_timing_state) quantiles_timing_in_ms_array
FROM tinybird.pipe_stats
where pipe_id = &#x27;PIPE_ID&#x27;
group by date
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>See <a href="/docs/sql-reference/functions/aggregate-functions#aggregate-function-combinators">Combinators</a> to learn more about the <code>-Merge</code> combinator.</p></div></div><h2 id="organization-service-data-sources" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Organization service data sources<a class="headerlink" href="#organization-service-data-sources" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>The following is a complete list of available Organization Service data sources:</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>organization.workspaces</code></td><td>Lists all Organization workspaces and related information, including name, IDs, databases, plan, when it was created, and whether it has been soft-deleted.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.processed_data</code></td><td>Information related to all processed data per day per workspace.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.datasources_storage</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.datasources_storage but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.pipe_stats</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.pipe_stats but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.pipe_stats_rt</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.pipe_stats_rt but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.datasources_ops_log</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.datasources_ops_log but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.data_transfer</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.data_transfer but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.jobs_log</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.jobs_log but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.sinks_ops_log</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.sinks_ops_log but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.bi_stats</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.bi_stats but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.bi_stats_rt</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.bi_stats_rt but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.endpoint_errors</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.endpoint_errors but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.shared_infra_active_minutes</code></td><td>Contains information about vCPU active minutes consumption aggregated by minute for all Organization workspaces. Only available for Developer and SaaS plans in shared infrastructure.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.shared_infra_qps_overages</code></td><td>Contains information about QPS consumption and overages aggregated by second for all Organization workspaces. Only available for Developer and SaaS plans in shared infrastructure.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.llm_usage</code></td><td>Equivalent to tinybird.llm_usage but with data for all Organization workspaces.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.backups</code></td><td>Contains backup metadata for dedicated clusters in the organization, including size and status.</td></tr><tr><td><code>organization.private_link</code></td><td>Contains Private Link usage and cost data for observability, associated with your organization&#x27;s workspaces.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><p>To query Organization Service data sources, go to any workspace that belongs to the Organization and use the previous as regular Service data source from the Playground or within pipes. Use the admin <code>Token of an Organization Admin</code>. You can also copy your admin Token and make queries using your preferred method, like <code>tb sql</code>.</p><h3 id="metrics-logs-service-data-source" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">metrics_logs service data source<a class="headerlink" href="#metrics-logs-service-data-source" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The <code>metrics_logs</code> Service data source is available in all the organization&#x27;s workspaces. As with the rest of Organization Service data sources, it&#x27;s only available to Organization administrators. New records for each of the metrics monitored are added every minute with the following schema:</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-warning text-error"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12 1.25C6.063 1.25 1.25 6.063 1.25 12S6.063 22.75 12 22.75 22.75 17.937 22.75 12 17.937 1.25 12 1.25M2.75 12A9.25 9.25 0 0 1 12 2.75c2.284 0 4.376.828 5.99 2.2l-.02.02-13 13-.02.02A9.2 9.2 0 0 1 2.75 12m3.26 7.05A9.25 9.25 0 0 0 19.05 6.01l-.019.02-13 13z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>The <code>metrics_logs</code> Service Data Source is only populated for Organizations with <strong>dedicated infrastructure</strong>. It contains hardware-level measurements (CPU, memory, disk) of dedicated cluster nodes. If your Organization is on shared infrastructure, this table is empty. For monitoring on shared infrastructure, use other Service Data Sources like <code>datasources_ops_log</code>, <code>pipe_stats</code>, and <code>datasources_storage</code>.</p></div></div><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>timestamp</td><td>DateTime</td><td>Timestamp of the metric</td></tr><tr><td>cluster</td><td>LowCardinality(String)</td><td>Name of the cluster</td></tr><tr><td>host</td><td>LowCardinality(String)</td><td>Name of the host</td></tr><tr><td>metric</td><td>LowCardinality(String)</td><td>Name of the metric</td></tr><tr><td>value</td><td>String</td><td>Value of the metric</td></tr><tr><td>description</td><td>LowCardinality(String)</td><td>Description of the metric</td></tr><tr><td>organization_id</td><td>String</td><td>ID of your organization</td></tr></tbody></table></div><p>The available metrics are the following:</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Metric</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>MemoryTracking</td><td>Total amount of memory, in bytes, allocated by the server.</td></tr><tr><td>OSMemoryTotal</td><td>The total amount of memory on the host system, in bytes.</td></tr><tr><td>InstanceType</td><td>Instance type of the host.</td></tr><tr><td>Query</td><td>Number of executing queries.</td></tr><tr><td>NumberCPU</td><td>Number of CPUs.</td></tr><tr><td>LoadAverage1</td><td>The whole system load, averaged with exponential smoothing over 1 minute. The load represents<!-- --> <!-- -->the number of threads across all the processes (the scheduling entities of the OS kernel), that<!-- --> <!-- -->are currently running by CPU or waiting for IO, or ready to run but not being scheduled at this<!-- --> <!-- -->point of time. This number includes all the processes, not only the server. The number<!-- --> <!-- -->can be greater than the number of CPU cores, if the system is overloaded, and many processes are<!-- --> <!-- -->ready to run but waiting for CPU or IO.</td></tr><tr><td>LoadAverage15</td><td>The whole system load, averaged with exponential smoothing over 15 minutes. The load represents<!-- --> <!-- -->the number of threads across all the processes (the scheduling entities of the OS kernel), that<!-- --> <!-- -->are currently running by CPU or waiting for IO, or ready to run but not being scheduled at this<!-- --> <!-- -->point of time. This number includes all the processes, not only the server. The number<!-- --> <!-- -->can be greater than the number of CPU cores, if the system is overloaded, and many processes are<!-- --> <!-- -->ready to run but waiting for CPU or IO.</td></tr><tr><td>CPUUsage</td><td>The ratio of time the CPU core was running OS kernel (system) code or userspace code. This is a<!-- --> <!-- -->system-wide metric, it includes all the processes on the host machine, not just the<!-- --> <!-- -->server. This includes also the time when the CPU was under-utilized due to the<!-- --> <!-- -->reasons internal to the CPU (memory loads, pipeline stalls, branch mispredictions, running<!-- --> <!-- -->another SMT core).</td></tr><tr><td>ReplicasSumQueueSize</td><td>Sum queue size (in the number of operations like get, merge) across Replicated tables.</td></tr><tr><td>ReplicasSumMergesInQueue</td><td>Sum of merge operations in the queue (still to be applied) across Replicated tables.</td></tr><tr><td>ReplicasSumInsertsInQueue</td><td>Sum of insert operations in the queue (still to be applied) across Replicated tables.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></article><div class="flex items-center justify-end h-10" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="italic text-caption"><span>Updated<!-- --> <time dateTime="2026-03-04T18:44:08.000Z">5 days ago</time></span></div></div><nav class="flex justify-between items-stretch gap-2 md:gap-4 mt-4
